defined_text = {
	name = sat_network_traffic_mil
	text = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { var_sat_network_traffic_mil > 1 }
		}
		localization_key = sat_network_traffic_mil_R
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { var_sat_network_traffic_mil < 1.01 }
		}
		localization_key = sat_network_traffic_mil_G
	}
}

### satellite gui window trigger tooltips ###

defined_text = {
	name = GNSS_MIL_BUTTON_WINDOW_TT_loc
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { GNSS_satellite_array^i > global.GNSS_sat_system_min_array^i }
				check_variable = { i = 0 }
			}
		}
		localization_key = GNSS_MIL_BUTTON_WINDOW_TT_yes
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { GNSS_satellite_array^i > global.GNSS_sat_system_min_array^i } }
				NOT = { check_variable = { i = 0 } }
			}
		}
		localization_key = GNSS_MIL_BUTTON_WINDOW_TT_no
	}
}
defined_text = {
	name = GNSS_CIV_BUTTON_WINDOW_TT_loc
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { GNSS_satellite_array^i > global.GNSS_sat_system_min_array^i }
				check_variable = { i = 0 }
			}
		}
		localization_key = GNSS_CIV_BUTTON_WINDOW_TT_yes
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { GNSS_satellite_array^i > global.GNSS_sat_system_min_array^i } }
				NOT = { check_variable = { i = 0 } }
			}
		}
		localization_key = GNSS_CIV_BUTTON_WINDOW_TT_no
	}
}

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { COM_satellite_array^i > global.COM_sat_system_min_array^i } }
				NOT = { check_variable = { i = 0 } }
			}
		}
		localization_key = COM_MIL_BUTTON_WINDOW_TT_no
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = total_sat_num_loc
	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:orbit_selected_TAG = {
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp = {
						value = var_GNSS_sat_total
						add = var_COM_sat_total
						add = var_SPY_sat_total
						add = var_KILL_sat_total
					}
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = "[?temp1]"
	}
}

		localization_key = GNSS_sat_total_loc_key

		trigger = {
			check_variable = { spp_payload_display_array^i > 999 }

	}

	name = call_missile_localization_utility_loc
